function crmCookieCleansing()
{
	var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
	var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
	var nofCRMCookies=0;
	for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++)
	{
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
		{
			c = c.substring(1);
		}
		if (c.indexOf("crm=") == 0)
		{
//console.log("found #"+nofCRMCookies+" "+c);
			nofCRMCookies++;
		}		
	}
	
	if ( nofCRMCookies > 1 )
	{
		console.log("crm:cookie de-duplication");
		var cookieString = 'crm=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;domain=secure.kilkennyormonde.com;path=/;SameSite=None;Secure';	
		document.cookie = cookieString;
		console.log("crm:cookie="+cookieString );
	}
}

crmCookieCleansing();

<script language="javascript">
// Move checkout JS
$(document).ready(function(){
	var flipClassTimeout
	// Show dragg handler on mds hover 
	$('#section_mainpage').on('mouseover', '.mdatd', function(){
		clearTimeout(flipClassTimeout);
		$(this).parent().parent().find('.checkoutMove').addClass('flipHandler');
	});
	// hide dragg handler on mouseOut from mda window
	$('#section_mainpage').on('mouseout', '.mdatd', function(){
		// avvoiding removing class when tooltip available, otherwise class was added and removed constantly
		flipClassTimeout = setTimeout(function(){
			$('.checkoutMove').removeClass('flipHandler');
		}, 100);
	});
});

Array.max = function(array) { return Math.max.apply(Math, array); };
Array.min = function(array) { return Math.min.apply(Math, array); };

function bindMDAFunctions()
{
	
	var pt = 'Price @PT@';
var pricetypes = [];
pricetypes['pr'] = 'per @ACCOMTYPE@';
pricetypes['pa'] = 'per adult';
var pp = 'Total package price, @PP@ night stay';
var nlpr = 'Price per @ACCOMTYPE@, based on @NLPR@ adults sharing';
var discount = 'Book Now and save <b>@DISCOUNT@%</b>';
var minlosstr = 'Minimum stay @MINLOS@ nights';
var invocc = 'Not avaliable for selected occupancy';
var nr = 'Only <b>@NUM_ROOMS@ @ACCOMTYPE@</b> remaining';
var nr1 = 'Only <b>1 @ACCOMTYPE@</b> remaining';
var poa = 'Price per night based on a @NIGHTS@ night stay';
var fixedlos = '@NIGHTS@ night stay';
var nocheckinprice = 'Price @PRICE@ @PT@';
var userdiscount = 'Discount applied';
var accomtypes = {'room':'room', 'house':'house', 'apartment':'apartment', 'experience':'experience', 'lodge':'lodge', 'villa':'villa', 'chalet':'chalet', 'cabin':'cabin', 'suite':'suite', 'pod':'pod', 'tourer':'tourer', 'cottage':'cottage'};
var accomtypesp = {'room':'rooms', 'house':'houses', 'apartment':'apartments', 'experience':'experiences', 'lodge':'lodges', 'villa':'villas', 'chalet':'chalets', 'cabin':'cabins', 'suite':'suites', 'pod':'pods', 'tourer':'tourers', 'cottage':'cottages'};
function mdaMouseEnter(mdaobj)
{
	//console.log(mdaobj.find('.ui-droppable-active').length);
	if(mdaobj.find('.ui-droppable-active').length == 0)
		mdaobj.addClass('mdahl');

		var re = mdaobj.attr('rel');
		if(re != '') {
			var obj = eval('(' + re + ')');

			var at = accomtypes.room;
			var atp = accomtypesp.room;
			if(obj.at)
			{
				at = accomtypes[obj.at];
				atp = accomtypesp[obj.at];
			}

			var id=mdaobj.attr('id');
			var p=id.split('_');
			var mbprefix = '';
			var rateroom, thisindex;
			if(p[0] == 'mb')
			{
				mbprefix = 'mb_';
				rateroom=p[1]+'_'+p[2]+'_'+p[3]+'_';
				thisindex=parseInt(p[4]);
			}
			else
			{
				rateroom=p[0]+'_'+p[1]+'_';
				thisindex=parseInt(p[2]);
			}

			if(obj.pp)
			{
				for(var i=1;(i<obj.pp && i<32);i++)
				{
					var n=thisindex+i;
					var m=rateroom+n.toString();
					var p='price_'+rateroom+n.toString();
					$('#'+mbprefix+m).addClass('mdahl');
					$('#'+p).addClass('contenthidden');
				}
			}
			if(obj.poa)
			{
				for(var i=1;(i<obj.nights && i<32);i++)
				{
					var n=thisindex+i;
					var m=rateroom+n.toString();
					var p='price_'+rateroom+n.toString();
					$('#'+mbprefix+m).addClass('mdahl');
					$('#'+p).addClass('contenthidden');
				}
			}
			else if(obj.los)
			{
				// highlight blocks for minlos, dont hide prices
				var los = obj.los.split(',');
				minlos = Math.min.apply(null,los);
				for(var i=1;i<minlos;i++)
				{
					var n=thisindex+i;
					var m=rateroom+n.toString();
					var p='price_'+rateroom+n.toString();
					if( ! $('#'+mbprefix+m).closest('.fwtable').hasClass('grabbingDates'))
						$('#'+mbprefix+m).addClass('mdahl');
				}
			}
			else if(obj.minlos)
			{
				var minlos = parseInt(obj.minlos);
				for(var i=1;i<minlos;i++)
				{
					var n=thisindex+i;
					var m=rateroom+n.toString();
					$('#'+mbprefix+m).addClass('mdahl');
				}
			}

			var a = [];

			if(obj.invocc)
				a.push(invocc);

			if(obj.d)
				a.push(userdiscount);

			if(true && mdaobj.is("[data-dis]"))
				a.push(discount.replace('@DISCOUNT@', mdaobj.attr('data-dis')));

			if(true && obj.discount) a.push(discount.replace('@DISCOUNT@', obj.discount));
			if((obj.nr) && obj.nr > 0 && obj.nr <= 5)
			{
				if(obj.nr == 1)
				{
					var prr=nr1.replace('@ACCOMTYPE@', at);
					a.push(prr);
				}
				else
				{
					var prr=nr.replace('@ACCOMTYPE@', atp);
					a.push(prr.replace('@NUM_ROOMS@', obj.nr));
				}
			}

			if(mdaobj.is("[data-pb]"))
			{
				var pb = mdaobj.attr('data-pb');
				var mpt;
				if(pb == 'pa') mpt = 'pa';
				else if(pb == 'pr') mpt = 'pr';
				if(mpt == 'pa' || mpt == 'pr')
				{
					if(true)
					{
						var ptprompt = pt.replace('@PT@', pricetypes[mpt]);
						ptprompt = ptprompt.replace('@ACCOMTYPE@', at);
						if(obj.fixedlos && !obj.pp)
							ptprompt += ', ' + fixedlos.replace('@NIGHTS@', obj.fixedlos);
						a.push(ptprompt);
					}
				}
				else
				{
					if(true) {
						var parts = pb.split(':');
						nlpr=nlpr.replace('@ACCOMTYPE@', at);
						a.push(nlpr.replace('@NLPR@', parts[1]));
					}
				}
			}

			if(obj.poa == true)
			{
				if(false && obj.nights)
				{
					a.push(poa.replace('@NIGHTS@', obj.nights));
				}
			}
			else
			{
				if(true && obj.pt && ! obj.nlpr)
				{
					var ptprompt = pt.replace('@PT@', pricetypes[obj.pt]);
					ptprompt = ptprompt.replace('@ACCOMTYPE@', at);
					if(obj.fixedlos && !obj.pp)
						ptprompt += ', ' + fixedlos.replace('@NIGHTS@', obj.fixedlos);
					a.push(ptprompt);
				}
				if(true && obj.pp) a.push(pp.replace('@PP@', obj.pp));
				if(true && obj.nlpr) a.push(nlpr.replace('@NLPR@', obj.nlpr));
				if(true && obj.los && !obj.pp && !obj.fixedlos) {
					var los = obj.los.split(',');
					minlos = Math.min.apply(null,los);
					if(minlos > 1) a.push(minlosstr.replace('@MINLOS@', minlos));
				}
			}
			if(true && a.length > 0)
			{
				var item = document.getElementById(mdaobj.attr('id'));
				var left = getItemXPosition(item);
				var top = getItemYPosition(item);
				$('#helpdiv').html(a.join('<br/>'));
				$('#helpdiv').css('left', left+15);
				$('#helpdiv').css('top', top+mdaobj.height() + 8);
				$('#helpdiv').css('visibility','hidden');
				$('#helpdiv').show();
				var maxx = getMaxXPosition('helpdiv','ipulserqh');
				var cx = parseInt($('#helpdiv').css('left'));
				if(cx > maxx)
					$('#helpdiv').css('left', maxx);
				$('#helpdiv').css('visibility','visible');
			}
		}
}
function mdaMouseLeave(mdaobj)
{
	$('.mdahl').not('.mdahlperm').removeClass('mdahl');
	$('#helpdiv').hide();
	$('.contenthidden').removeClass('contenthidden');
}
$(document).ready(function() {
$('.no-touch .mdasel').hover(function() { mdaMouseEnter($(this)) }, function() { mdaMouseLeave($(this)) });

	$('.nocheckin').hover(function() {
		var re = $(this).attr('rel');
		var obj = eval('(' + re + ')');
		var a = [];
		if(obj.nocheckin)	a.push('No check in possible, stay through only');
		var at = accomtypes.room;
		if(obj.at)
			at = accomtypes[obj.at];
		if(obj.price)
		{
			var price = parseFloat( obj.price );
			var exrate = parseFloat( $( '#currencymul' ).val() );
			if( exrate !== 1 )
			{
				var v1 =  price * exrate;
				v1 = Math.floor( v1 * 100.0 ) / 100.0;
				price = v1;
			}
			if( roundMDAPrices )
				price = price.toFixed( 0 );
			else
				price = price.toFixed( 2 );
			var currencysymbol = $( '#currency_symbol' ).val();
			price = currencysymbol + price;
			var str = nocheckinprice.replace('@PRICE@', price);
			str = str.replace('@PT@', pricetypes[obj.pt]);
			str = str.replace('@ACCOMTYPE@', at);
			a.push(str);
		}
		if(true && true && a.length > 0)
		{
			var item = document.getElementById($(this).attr('id'));
			var left = getItemXPosition(item);
			var top = getItemYPosition(item);
			$('#helpdiv').html(a.join('<br/>'));
			$('#helpdiv').css('left', left+15);
			$('#helpdiv').css('top', top+$(this).height() + 8);
			$('#helpdiv').show();
			var maxx = getMaxXPosition('helpdiv','ipulserqh');
			var cx = parseInt($('#helpdiv').css('left'));
			if(cx > maxx)
				$('#helpdiv').css('left', maxx);
			$('#helpdiv').css('visibility','visible');
		}
	},
	function() {
		$('#helpdiv').hide();
	});
});
	
	

	bindMDAFunctions.mdaMouseEnter = mdaMouseEnter;
	bindMDAFunctions.mdaMouseLeave = mdaMouseLeave;
}
function bindTooltipFunctions()
{
	$('.hastooltip').hover(function() {
		if( $.trim( $(this).attr( 'data-tooltip' ) ) === '' ) return;

		var a = [];
		a.push($(this).attr('data-tooltip'));
		if(a.length <= 0) return;

		var offsetx = 0;
		var offsety = 0;
		var top;
		var handled = false;
		var item = document.getElementById($(this).attr('id'));
		if(container = $(this).attr('data-container'))
		{
			// if using tooltips in a popup, set data-container so that we can calculate the position
			// relative to the container popup
			if(container == 'popupdiv' || container == 'popupcontent_room')
			{
				var ipulsePosition = $('#ipulse').offset();
				var ipulseLeft = ipulsePosition.left;
				var ipulseTop = ipulsePosition.top;

				var popupPos = $('#' + container).position();
				var leftDistance = popupPos.left + parseInt($('#' + container).css('margin-left'));
				var topDistance = popupPos.top + parseInt($('#' + container).css('margin-top'));
				leftDistance -= ipulseLeft;
				topDistance -= ipulseTop;

				if(parent = $(this).attr('data-parent')) {
					var parentPos = $('#' + parent).position();
					leftDistance += parentPos.left + parseInt($('#' + parent).css('margin-left')) ;
					topDistance += parentPos.top + parseInt($('#' + parent).css('margin-top'));
				}


				var thisPos = $(this).position();		// position relative to top-left of popup container
				var thisLeft = thisPos.left, thisTop = thisPos.top;

				var scrollLeft = $(document).scrollLeft();
				var scrollTop = $(document).scrollTop();

				offsetx = (leftDistance + thisLeft) + scrollLeft + 5;
				offsety = (topDistance + thisTop) + scrollTop + $(this).height() + 5;

				$('#helpdiv').css('left', offsetx);
				$('#helpdiv').css('top', offsety);
				handled = true;
			}
			else
			{
				var i = document.getElementById(container);
				offsetx = getItemXPosition(i) - getItemXPosition(item);
				offsety = getItemYPosition(i) - getItemYPosition(item);
			}
		}

		if( $(this).attr( 'data-tooltip-offsetx' ) ) offsetx = offsetx + parseInt( $(this).attr( 'data-tooltip-offsetx' ) );
		if( $(this).attr( 'data-tooltip-offsety' ) ) offsety = offsety + parseInt( $(this).attr( 'data-tooltip-offsety' ) );

		if(handled == false)
		{
			var left = getItemXPosition(item);
			var top = getItemYPosition(item);

			$('#helpdiv').css('left', offsetx+left+5);
			$('#helpdiv').css('top', offsety+top+($(this).height()+5));
		}

		var html = a.join( '<br/>' );

		if( $( '#currency' ).length > 0 && $( '#cursel_' + $('#currency').val() ).length > 0 )
		{
			var currency = $('#currency').val();
			var currencyElement = $( '#cursel_' + $('#currency').val() );

			var currencySymbol = getCurrencySymbol( currency );

			var exchangeRate = currencyElement.data( 'conversionrate' );
			var rounding = currencyElement.data( 'rounding' );

			html = changeCurrencyValue( '.curdis', exchangeRate, rounding, html );

			html = $('<div />',{ html: html } );

			if( currencySymbol )
				html.find( '._cs' ).html( currencySymbol );
			else
				html.find( '._cs' ).html( '' );

			html = html.html();
		}

		$('#helpdiv').html( html );
		$('#helpdiv').css('visibility','hidden');
		$('#helpdiv').show();
		var maxx = getMaxXPosition('helpdiv','ipulserqh');
		var cx = parseInt($('#helpdiv').css('left'));
		if(cx > (maxx-50))
			$('#helpdiv').css('left', maxx-50);
		$('#helpdiv').css('visibility','visible');
	},
	function() {
		$('#helpdiv').hide();
	});

	$('.hasroomtooltip').hover(function() {

		var tooltip = document.getElementById("tooltip_" + $(this).attr('id'));
		var placeholder = String($(this).data('tooltip'));
		tooltip.innerHTML = placeholder;
		tooltip.style.display = "inline-block";

	}, function() {

 		var tooltip = document.getElementById("tooltip_" + $(this).attr('id'));
		tooltip.style.display = "none";

	});

}

function docReady()
{
	var p = $('#partya').val();
	var show = true;
	var pp = p.split(';');
	for(var i=0; i<pp.length; i++)
	{
		var ppp = pp[i].split(',');
		for(var j=0; j<ppp.length; j++)
		{
			if(ppp[j] != 0)
			{
				show = false;
				break;
			}
		}
	}

	if(show && false) {
		setTimeout(function() {
			$( document ).trigger( 'showRoomPartySelection' );
		}, 0 );
	}

	$(document).trigger('avvioDocReadyEarly');
	// replace with calling initEvents (part of ReviewProWidget)
	if(typeof initEvents == 'function') initEvents();

	$('.contentboxtwoline .expander').expander({'slicePoint': 195, 'expandText': 'read more', 'userCollapseText': 'show less'});
	$('.contentboxthreeline .expander').expander({'slicePoint': 300, 'expandText': 'read more', 'userCollapseText': 'show less'});

	bindMDAFunctions();
	bindTooltipFunctions();

	updateFilters('docready');

	$('.mdabox').click(function() { changeCheckin($(this)); });
	$('.sdabutton').click(function() { sdaClick($(this)); });
	$('.multiroombutton').click(function() { multiRoomClick($(this)); });

	avvioUpdateScroll();
	$('.roomlink').click(function() { toggleRoom($(this)); });
	$('.ratelink').click(function() { toggleRate($(this)); });

	$('.mrsel').change(function() {
		// multi-room booking radio buttons
		$('.sdacontainer-mrp').addClass('sdacontainer-notselected-mr');
		var p = $(this).val().split('_');
		var rateID = p[0]; var roomID = p[1];
		var total = 0;
		$('.mrsel').each(function() {
			var ip = $(this).val().split('_');
			var ir = ip[0];
			if(ir == rateID && $(this).is(':checked'))
			{
				var idpart = $(this).attr('id').split('_');
				var divid = idpart[1]+'_'+idpart[3]+'_'+idpart[2];
				$('#mrp_'+divid).removeClass('sdacontainer-notselected-mr');
				total += parseFloat($(this).attr('data-price-eur'));
			}
		});
		total=total.toFixed(2);
		var localtotal = total*$('#currencymul').val();
		localtotal = formatCurrency(localtotal.toFixed(2));

		var nights = Math.max( parseInt( $( '#nights' ).val() ), 1 );
		$('#mrprcontainer_'+rateID).html('<span class="curdis" data-curr="'+ ( total / nights ).toFixed(2) +'" data-rounding="2">'+ formatCurrency( ( localtotal / nights ).toFixed(2) ) +'</span>');
		$('#mrcontainer_'+rateID).html('<span id="mbprice_'+rateID+'_xxx_12" class="curdis" data-curr="'+total+'" data-rounding="2">'+localtotal+'</span>');
		if($('#clickrateroom').val() != '')
		{
			$('#forceStart').val($('#MDAWindowStart').val());
			startLoading();
			$('#reloadType').val('partial');
			jsrAction('refreshprices');		// we only need to refresh if there was a visible rateroom clicked on mda
		}
		else {
			jsrAction('continuelos');		// we need to get this refreshed
		}
	});

	var numberOfMonths = 1;
	if( $( '.media-query-indicator' ).first().css( 'z-index' ) == 0 ) numberOfMonths = 2;
	
	$('.membersignup').click(function() {
		handleMemberRatesButton();
	});
	$( '#ipulse' ).on( 'click', '.membersignupPopup', function() {
		handleMemberRatesButton('fromPopup');
	});

	if(true)
		setupDragDrop();

	$(document).trigger('avvioDocReadyLate');
}

function setupDragDrop()
{
	$(".no-touch .itemprices tr").each(function(){
		$(this).find(".mda-search-highlight .checkoutMove").last().show();
	}); 
	
	$(".checkoutMove").draggable({
		stop: function(event, ui){
			$('.mdabox.mda-search-highlightOriginal').addClass('mda-search-highlight');
		},
		snap: ".checkoutMoveSnap",
		snapMode: "inner",
		axis: "x",
		revert: true,
		revertDuration: 0,
		snapTolerance: 40,
	});
	$(".checkoutMoveSnapWrapper").droppable({
		activate: function(){
			$("#dragAndDropCheckoutDate").val(1);
			$(this).parent().addClass("grabbing");
			$(".checkoutMoveSnapDisabled").css("opacity", 1);
			$(".hideWhenDragging").css("opacity", 0);
			$(this).closest('.fwtable').addClass('grabbingDates');
			$(this).closest('tr').find('td > div').removeClass('mdahl');
		},
		deactivate: function(){
			$(".grabbing").removeClass("grabbing");
			$(".mda-search-highlightTemp").removeClass("mda-search-highlight");
			$(".checkoutMoveSnapDisabled").css("opacity", 0);
			$(".hideWhenDragging").css("opacity", 1);
			$("#dragAndDropCheckoutDate").val(0);
			$('.grabbingDates').removeClass('grabbingDates');
		},
		drop: function(event, ui) {
			newCheckout = this.id;
			var clickedID = this.id;
			kkLOS = $("#"+this.id).attr("data-drag-los");
			$("#nights").val(kkLOS);
			newCheckout = newCheckout.split("_");
			newCheckout = newCheckout[1].split("-");
			$(".ui-datepicker-calendar td").each(function(index){
				if($(this).attr("data-year") == newCheckout[0] && $(this).attr("data-month") == (newCheckout[1] - 1))
				{
					if(parseInt($(this).find("a").html()) == parseInt(newCheckout[2]))
					{
						if($("#"+clickedID).attr("data-column-number") < 6)
							$("#forceStart").val($("#MDAWindowStart").val());
						changeCheckout();
					}
				}
			});
		},
		over: function(event, ui) {
			if( ! $(this).closest(".mdabox, .mda").hasClass("mda-search-highlight"))
				$(this).closest(".mdabox, .mda").addClass("mda-search-highlight mda-search-highlightTemp");
				
			$(this).closest(".mdatd").next().children(".mda-search-highlight").removeClass("mda-search-highlight");
			$(this).closest(".mdatd").next().next().children(".mda-search-highlight").removeClass("mda-search-highlight");
			$(this).closest(".mdatd").next().next().next().children(".mda-search-highlight").removeClass("mda-search-highlight");
			$(this).closest(".mdatd").next().next().next().next().children(".mda-search-highlight").removeClass("mda-search-highlight");
		},
	});
}

function handleMemberRatesButton( usecase )
{
	usecase = (typeof usecase !== 'undefined') ? usecase : '';
	var delayTimer = 0;
	if(usecase == 'fromPopup')
	{
		$('#popupdiv').fadeOut('fast');
		lightsOn();
		delayTimer = 500;
	}
	setTimeout(function() {
		var ms = $('.member-rate-signup').length;
		if(ms >= 1) {
			$('#hideClosedRates').val(0);
			$('#section_closedsignup').slideDown(100);
			$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $( '#section_closedsignup').offset().top - 150 }, 500 );
			$('#useremail').focus(); 
		}
		else {
			$('.top-filter-profile').trigger('click');
			$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $( '#top-filter-profile-label').offset().top - 20 }, 500 );
		}
	}, delayTimer);
}

function formatCurrency(num)
{
	var num_parts = num.toString().split(".");
	num_parts[0] = num_parts[0].replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ",");
	return num_parts.join(".");
}

{
	updateDisplayThumbContainer();
	$(document).trigger('avvioDocReadyEarly');
      $('.popupcontent').expander({'slicePoint': 250, 'expandText': 'read more', 'userCollapseText': 'show less'});

      }
            
      $('.imageselector').click(function() {                      
            var p = $(this).attr('id').split('_');

      {
      	showVideoThumbnails();
	  }

      $(this).addClass('rplink_active');
		$('#popup-panel-information').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-3d').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-images').show();
		$('#popup-panel-videos').hide();
		updateDisplayThumbContainer();
	});
	$('#room-video-icon').click(function() {
		$('.rplink_active').removeClass('rplink_active');
		$('.rplink_inactive').removeClass('rplink_inactive');
		$('#popup-tab').removeClass('info-tab-selected');
      $(this).addClass('rplink_active');
		$('#popup-panel-information').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-3d').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-images').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-videos').show();
	});
	$('#room-3d-icon').click(function() {
		$('.rplink_active').removeClass('rplink_active');
		$('.rplink_inactive').removeClass('rplink_inactive');
		$('#popup-tab').removeClass('info-tab-selected');
      $(this).addClass('rplink_active');
		$('#popup-panel-information').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-3d').show();
		$('#popup-panel-images').hide();
		$('#popup-panel-videos').hide();
	});
	$(document).trigger('avvioDocReadyLate');

	if(openMatterportTab){
		$("#room-3d-icon").click();
		openMatterportTab = false;
	}
}

function updateDisplayThumbContainer()
{
	$('#popup-thumb-container').css('display','block');
	if($('#popup-thumb-container').width() < $('#popup-thumb-mask').width())
		$('#popup-thumb-container').css('display','contents');
}
function slideThumbnails(index)
{
	updateDisplayThumbContainer();
	var sliderMaskWidth = $('#popup-thumb-mask').width();
	var sliderContainerWidth = $('#popup-thumb-container').width();

	if(sliderMaskWidth >= sliderContainerWidth)
		return;

	var positionLeft = $('#popup-thumb-container').position().left;
	var thumbWidth = $('.cycler_thumb').first().outerWidth(true);
	var visibleThumbs = Math.floor(sliderMaskWidth / 2 / thumbWidth);
	var containerLeftPosition;
	if(index > visibleThumbs)
	{
		containerLeftPosition = thumbWidth * (index - visibleThumbs);
		containerLeftPosition = -Math.min(sliderContainerWidth - sliderMaskWidth, containerLeftPosition);
		
	}else
		containerLeftPosition = Math.max((positionLeft - thumbWidth), 0);
	
	$('#popup-thumb-container').css('left', containerLeftPosition + 'px');
}
function cycleImages(index)
{
      var $active = $('#cycler .active');     
      
      if(index == -100)
            var $next = ($active.next().length > 0) ? $active.next() : $('#cycler img:first');
      else
      {
            var $next = $('#imagesequence_'+index);
            clearInterval(imagecycletimeout); 
      }
      var p = $next.attr('id').split('_');     
      $('.imageselselected').removeClass('imageselselected');
      $('#imageselector_'+p[1]).parent().addClass('imageselselected');
      currentselection = p[1];
      $next.css('z-index',2);//move the next image up the pile
      $active.fadeOut(600,function() { //fade out the top image
            $active.css('z-index',1).show().removeClass('active');//reset the z-index and unhide the image
            $next.css('z-index',3).addClass('active');//make the next image the top one
      });
	slideThumbnails(p[1]);
}
function cycleNext()
{
	clearInterval(imagecycletimeout);
	var $active = $("#cycler .active");
	var $next = ($active.next().length > 0) ? $active.next() : $("#cycler img:first");
	var p = $next.attr("id").split("_");
	cycleImages(p[1]);
	imagecycletimeout = setInterval("cycleImages(-100)", 4000);
}
function cyclePrev()
{
	clearInterval(imagecycletimeout);
	var $active = $('#cycler img.active');
	var $prev = ($active.prev('img').length > 0) ? $active.prev('img') : $('#cycler img:last');
	var p = $prev.attr('id').split('_');
	cycleImages(p[1]);
	imagecycletimeout = setInterval('cycleImages(-100)', 4000);
}
$(document).ready(function(){
	$('#mainarea').on('click', '#kkCyclerArrowRight', function(){
		cycleNext();
	});
	$('#mainarea').on('click', '#cycler img.imagesequence', function(){
		cycleNext();
	});
	$('#mainarea').on('click', '#kkCyclerArrowLeft', function(){
		cyclePrev();
	});
});

	});
}

function startLoading()
{
	$('#main-panel-cell').addClass('washed');
	$('.loader').css('visibility','visible');
}

function changeCheckin(obj)
{
	startLoading();
	var mdaopt = JSON.parse(obj.attr('data-mda'));
	var relopt = JSON.parse(obj.attr('rel'));

	if(relopt.pp)
	{
		$('#nights').val(relopt.pp);
	}
	else if(mdaopt.los)
	{
		var n = parseInt($('#nights').val());
		var l = [];
		for(var i = 1; i<=31; i++) {
			if(mdaopt.los & Math.pow(2,i-1)) {
				l.push(i);
			}
		}
		if($.inArray(n,l) == -1) {
			$('#nights').val(l[0]);
		}
	}

	var kkCheckinDate = new Date(mdaopt.date);
	var kkCheckoutDate = kkCheckinDate.addDays($('#nights').val());
	var kkStartDate = new Date($('#MDAWindowStart').val());
	var daysDifference = (kkCheckoutDate.getTime() - kkStartDate.getTime()) / (1000 * 3600 * 24);

	if(daysDifference < 7 && kkStartDate.getTime() !== kkCheckinDate.getTime())
		$('#forceStart').val($('#MDAWindowStart').val());

	$('#clickrateroom').val(mdaopt.rateID+','+mdaopt.roomID);
	if('party' in mdaopt)
	{
		var newval = mdaopt.rateID+'_'+mdaopt.roomID;
		$('#mrsel_'+mdaopt.rateID+'_'+mdaopt.party+'_'+mdaopt.roomID).prop('checked', true);
	}
	$('#start').val('');
	$('#checkin').val(mdaopt.date);
	$('#reloadType').val('partial');
	jsrAction('changeSearch');
}

Date.prototype.addDays = function(days) {
    var date = new Date(this.valueOf());
    date.setDate(date.getDate() + parseInt(days));
    return date;
}

function changeCheckout()
{
	$('#reloadType').val('partial');
	jsrAction('changeSearch');
}

function sdaClick(obj)
{
	var guestsURL = $('#guestsURL').val();
	var mdaopt = JSON.parse(obj.attr('data-mda'));
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__RATEID__', mdaopt.rateID);
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__CHECKIN__', mdaopt.date);
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__NIGHTS__', $('#nights').val());
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__ROOMID__', mdaopt.roomID);
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__CURRENCY__', $('#currency').val());
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__PARTY__', obj.data( 'party' ) );
	open(guestsURL, '_self');
}

function multiRoomClick(obj)
{
	var guestsURL = $('#guestsURL').val();
	var rateID = obj.attr('data-rateID');
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__RATEID__', rateID);
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__CHECKIN__', $('#checkin').val());
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__NIGHTS__', $('#nights').val());
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__PARTY__', obj.data( 'party' ) );

	var roomIDs = [];
	$('.mrsel').each(function() {
		var ip = $(this).val().split('_');
		var irate = ip[0];
		var iroom = ip[1];
		if(irate == rateID && $(this).is(':checked'))
			roomIDs.push(iroom);
	});

	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__ROOMID__', roomIDs.join(','));
	guestsURL = guestsURL.replace('__CURRENCY__', $('#currency').val());
	open(guestsURL, '_self');
}

function updateFilters(src)
{
	if(true) { newTripTease(); }
}

function newTripTease()
{
	$(".price-fighter-widget").remove()
	$('#section_tripTease').remove();

	var rateGroupsChecked = $('#ipulse .top-filter-container .top-filter-select-rategroups-rategroup input:checked').length;
	var roomGroupsChecked = $('#ipulse .top-filter-container .top-filter-select-roomgroups-roomgroup input:checked').length;
	if((rateGroupsChecked + roomGroupsChecked) > 0)
		return;

	$("body").append('<div id="section_tripTease"></div>');
	arg = avvioDisplayedPrices;
	try {
		clearTimeout(refreshTriptease);
	} catch(err) {
		//do nothing, refreshTriptease not defined
	}
	refreshTriptease = setTimeout(function() { jsrAction('tripTease',JSON.stringify(arg)) }, 1000);
}

function togglePriceSection(name, id)
{
	id = String(id);
	var ids;
	if($('#'+name).val() == '') ids = [];
	else ids = $('#'+name).val().split(',');
	var state = $('#explink_'+id).attr('data-state');
	if(state == 'visible')
	{
		ids.splice($.inArray(id, ids), 1);
		$('#itemprices_'+id).slideUp(100);
		$('#opt_button_prompt_'+id).text($('#opt_button_prompt_'+id).attr('data-collapsed'));
		$('#explink_'+id).attr( 'data-icon', 'chevron-down');
		$('#explink_'+id).attr('data-state', 'hidden');
		$('#opt_button_'+id).removeClass('actiontype-light');
	}
	else
	{
		ids.push(id);
		ids = $.unique(ids);
		$('#itemprices_'+id).slideDown(100);
		$('#opt_button_prompt_'+id).text($('#opt_button_prompt_'+id).attr('data-expanded'));
		$('#explink_'+id).attr( 'data-icon', 'chevron-up');
		$('#explink_'+id).attr('data-state', 'visible');
		$('#opt_button_'+id).addClass('actiontype-light');
	}
	if(ids.length == 0) $('#'+name).val('');
	else $('#'+name).val(ids.join(','));
}

function pushExp(name, id)
{
	id = String(id);
	var ids;
	if($('#'+name).val() == '') ids = [];
	else ids = $('#'+name).val().split(',');
	ids.push(id);
	ids = $.unique(ids);
	$('#'+name).val(ids.join(','));
}

function jsrAction(action,arg) 
{     
      $('#fw_jsrequest').val('formaction');
      $('#jsr_formaction').val(action);
      $('#jsr_formaction_arg').val(arg);
      doFormAction();
      $('#fw_jsrequest').val('');
      $('#jsr_formaction').val('');
      $('#jsr_formaction_arg').val(''); 
}

function doFormAction()
{
	if(ajaxrunning==1) return 1;
	$('.loading').css('visibility','visible');      
	ajaxrunning=1;
	$.ajax({          
		url: "https://secure.kilkennyormonde.com/convert/site/Kilkenny%20Ormonde%20Hotel/en/results.php",
		type: "post",   
		data: $('#searchdate').serialize(),
		error: function (result) {                  
			ajaxrunning=0;
		},

		success: function (result, textStatus, x) {
			$('.fw_asyncinputerror').removeClass('fw_inputerror');
			var obj={};
			if(result != '')
			{
				try
				{					
					var obj = JSON.parse(result);
				}
				catch(err) {
					console.log('error');
				}
			}
			if(obj._success)
			{
				var msg = '<div class="success">' + obj._success + '</div>';
				$('#async_message_container').html(msg);
			}                  
			if(obj._sections)  
			{
				if( ! (obj._success) && ( ! obj._errors))
					$('#async_message_container').html('');
				var sections = obj._sections;
				$.each(sections, function(i,v) {
					var content = obj._section[v];
					$('#section_'+v).html(content);                              
				});
			}
			if(obj._formerrors)
			{			
				$.each(obj._formerrors, function(k,v) {
					$('#'+v).addClass('fw_inputerror fw_asyncinputerror');
				});
			}
			if(obj._scroll && $('#'+obj._scroll).length > 0)
			{
				$('html, body').animate({
					scrollTop: $('#'+obj._scroll).offset().top - 100
				}, 500);
			}
			if(obj._highlight) {
                        $.each(obj._highlight, function(i,v) {
                        	$('#'+v).addClass('highlighting');
                        	$('#'+v).effect('highlight', {color:'#50497c'}, 1500, function() { $(this).removeClass('highlighting'); } );
				});
                  }
			if(obj._redirect)
				window.location=obj._redirect;
			if(obj._state)
			{
				var sObj = { "state": null, "message": "" };
				if(history.pushState) history.pushState(sObj, 'Page Title', obj._state);
			}
			if(obj._message)
				alert(obj._message);
			if(typeof avvioUpdateScrollMarker == 'function')
				avvioUpdateScrollMarker();
			if(obj._callback)
				window[obj._callback](obj);
			if( ! obj._type)			
			{				
				docReady();
				$('.non-scrolling').removeClass('non-scrolling');
			}
			else
				docReadyPopup();
			$('#fw_jsrequest').val('');
			if( ! obj._notDoneLoading)
			{
				$('.loading').css('visibility','hidden');
				$('.washed').removeClass('washed');
				$('.loader').css('visibility','hidden');
			}
			ajaxrunning=0;   

			if(typeof LazyLoadElement != 'undefined') {
				LazyLoadElement.update();
			}
		}
	});
}

function ISODateString(d)
{
	function pad(n){return n<10 ? '0'+n : n}
	return d.getUTCFullYear() + '-' + pad(d.getUTCMonth()+1) + '-' + pad(d.getUTCDate());
}

function moveStart(type)
{
	clearTimeout(refreshTriptease);
	var mdadates = [];
	var daycount = 0;
	$('.itemprices_mda').each(function() {
		if( ! $(this).is(':visible'))
			return true;
		$(this).find('.mtdch').each(function(k,v) {
			if($(this).is(':visible'))
			{
				mdadates.push($(this).attr('data-date'));
				daycount++;
			}
		});
		return false;
	});
	mdadates.sort();

	var arg;
	if(type == 'next')
		arg = mdadates[mdadates.length-1];
	else if(type == 'prev')
	{
		var d = new Date(mdadates[0]);
		d.setDate(d.getDate()-daycount);
		arg = ISODateString(d);
	}

	startLoading();
	$('#checkin').val('');
	$('#start').val(arg);
	$('#reloadType').val('partial');
	$('#lastaction').val('movestart');
	jsrAction('movestart', '{"start":"' + arg + '"}');
}

function popupLoader(type)
{
      lightsOff();      
      $('#helpdiv').hide();
      var dims;
      if(type == 'lospopup') dims = [800,400];
      else if(type == 'roominfo') dims = [800,700];
      else if(type == 'rateinfo') dims = [800,400];
      else if(type == 'partner') dims = [800,400]; 
      else if(type == 'waitlist') dims = [800,400];
      else if(type == 'threeDRedirect') dims = [400,200];
      if(lastpopuptype != type)
      {            
            var h = dims[1] / 2;
            var s = '<div class="popup_loading_big" style="width:'+dims[0]+'px;height:'+dims[1]+'px;text-align:center;font-size:26px;font-family:Open Sans;font-weight:100;line-height:'+h+'px;">';
            s += '<i class="fa fa-fw fa-refresh fa-spin"></i>Loading...';
            s += '</div>';            
            $('#section_popup_inner').html(s);
      }
      else
      {   
            $('#section_popup_inner').addClass('washed');
            $('.popup_loading').css('visibility','visible');
      }
      $('#popupdiv').css('margin-left', 0-(dims[0] / 2));
      $('#popupdiv').css('margin-top', 0-(dims[1] / 2));
      $('#popupdiv').show();
      lastpopuptype = type; 
}

      lightsOn();
}

/*detect scrollbar use start*/
var avvioXDirection = "";
var avvioYDirection = "";
 
var avvioOldX = 0;
var avvioOldY = 0;
var outOfView = false;
function getMouseDirection(e) {
    if (avvioOldX < e.pageX) {
        avvioXDirection = "right";
    } else {
        avvioXDirection = "left";
    }
    if (avvioOldY < e.pageY) {
        avvioYDirection = "down";
    } else {
        avvioYDirection = "up";
    } 
    avvioOldX = e.pageX;
    avvioOldY = e.pageY;
 }
var scrollbarUsed = false;
var mouseXLargerThanWindowWidth = function(mouseX){
	if( $(window).outerWidth() <= mouseX ){
		return true;
	}
}
$(document).scroll(function(e){
	if( outOfView ){
		scrollbarUsed = true;
	}
});
/*detect scrollbar use end*/
var alloraStage   = "no-booking";
var stopExitPopup = false;

function createCookie(key, value)
{
	var cookie = escape(key) + "=" + escape(value) + "; expires=Sat, 24 Dec 2022 09:25:09 UTC; path=/";
	document.cookie = cookie;
}

function readCookie(name)
{
	var key = name + "=";
	var cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
	for( var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++)
	{
		var cookie = cookies[i];
		while (cookie.charAt(0) === ' ')
		{
			cookie = cookie.substring(1,cookie.length);
		}
		if(cookie.indexOf(key) === 0)
		{
			return cookie.substring(key.length, cookie.length);
		}
	}
	return null;
}
$(document).ready(function()
{
	var bodyElement = document.body;
	bodyElement.addEventListener("mousemove", getMouseDirection, false);

	$('body').append('<div aria-hidden="true" id="exitIntentWrapper" class="exitIntentContainer exitPopupContainer  mediumFont rectangle size70 center alignCenter noFontChosen dark image"><div id="exitIntentCloseTrigger" class="exitIntentClose closePopup">X</div><div id="exitIntentModal" class="exitIntentModal pretendModal"></div><div id="exitIntentPopupContainer" class="exitIntentContent"><div id="exitIntentCloseTriggerInside" class="exitIntentClose closePopup">X</div><div id="allContent" class="allContentContainer"><div id="exitIntentHeading" class="exitIntentSpacing exitIntentTitle">We understand your plans might change!</div><div id="exitIntentText" class="exitIntentSpacing exitIntentDesc"><p><span style="font-size: medium;">Don&apos;t worry, we offer fully flexible cancellation policies in the event that your plans may change. You can change your booking, modify your booking or cancel your booking. Book direct and get the best rates and don&apos;t stress if your plans change.</span></p><p><span style="font-size: medium;">If you are not quite ready to complete your booking, leave us your email address and we will save your cart for you to return at a later time.</span></p><span style="font-size: medium;"><br></span><p><span style="color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: ProximaNovaRegular, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; text-align: justify; font-size: medium;"><label for="emailBasketAddressPopup" class="sr-only">Enter Email</label><input class="basketEmailInput" type="text" name="emailBasketAddressPopup" id="emailBasketAddressPopup" value="" placeholder="Enter Email" />&nbsp; <span class="exitIntentBtn sendBasketTrigger" data-click-state="" id="exitIntentCtaButton" data-target="emailBasketAddressPopup" >Send</span><div id="section_reportToUserPopup"></div></span></p></div><div id="exitIntentAction" class="exitIntentCta popupCta exitIntentSpacing"><a rel="noopener" class="exitIntentBtn" id="exitIntentCtaButton" target="_blank" href="https://ag.avvio.com/convert/site/Kilkenny%20Ormonde%20Hotel/en/results.php">View our Rates!</a></div></div></div></div>');
	var exitPopup = $('.exitIntentContainer');
	
	//leaving the viewport
	var clickTimer = null;
	$(document).on("mouseout", function(e)
	{
		var showTimer = 500;
		if(avvioXDirection == 'right' && mouseXLargerThanWindowWidth(e.clientX))
			showTimer = 2000;
		outOfView = true;

		e = e ? e : window.event;
		var from = e.relatedTarget || e.toElement;
		if ( (!from || from.nodeName === "HTML") )
		{
			clearTimeout(clickTimer);
			clickTimer = setTimeout(function()
			{
				if(!scrollbarUsed)
					showExitIntentPopup();
			}, showTimer);
			scrollbarUsed = false;
		}
	});
	//detect still mouse
	var timeout = null;
	$(document).on('mousemove', function()
	{
		clearTimeout(timeout);
		timeout = setTimeout(function()
		{
			showExitIntentPopup();
		}, 90000);
	});
	$('.exitIntentModal, .exitIntentClose, .exitIntentCloseAction').on('click',function(){
		$('.exitIntentContainer').hide();
	});
	$(document).on('keydown', function(event) {
		if ( event.key == "Escape" && $('.exitPopupContainer').css('display') == 'block' ) {
			$('.exitPopupContainer').hide();
		}
	});
	$('input').focusin( function() {
		stopExitPopup = true;
	});
	$('input').focusout( function() {
		stopExitPopup = false;
	});
	
});
function showExitIntentPopup()
{
	var noShow = ['pre-stay', 'post-stay'];
	if( typeof(alloraStage) == 'string' && noShow.includes(alloraStage) )
		return false;
	if( stopExitPopup )
		return false;

	if(readCookie("ExitIntentCookie_33") == null)
		showExitIntentPopupNow();
}
function showExitIntentPopupNow()
{
	createCookie("ExitIntentCookie_33", "33");
	$('.exitPopupContainer').show();
	document.getElementById("exitIntentPopupContainer").setAttribute("role", "alert");
}
$(function()
{
	var input = document.getElementById("emailBasketAddressPopup");
	if(input)
	{
		input.addEventListener("keyup", function(event)
		{
			if (event.keyCode === 13) {
				event.preventDefault();
				var btn = $('.sendBasketTrigger[data-target="emailBasketAddressPopup"]');
				btn.trigger('click');
			}
		});
	}
	var inputInline = document.getElementById("emailBasketAddress");
	if(inputInline)
	{
		inputInline.addEventListener("keyup", function(event)
		{
			if (event.keyCode === 13) {
				event.preventDefault();
				var btn = $('.sendBasketTrigger[data-target="emailBasketAddress"]');
				btn.trigger('click');
			}
		});
	}
	$('body').on('click','.sendBasketTrigger', function(){
		if( $(this).data('click-state') == 'clicked')
			return false;

		/*captcha code start*/
		var ele = document.getElementById( "humanCaptcha" );
		var atr = ele.getAttribute( "value" );
	
		document.getElementById("hOV_screenWidth").value = screen.width;
		document.getElementById("hOV_screenHeight").value = screen.height;

		var sum=0;
		for( var i=0; i<atr.length; i++ )
		{
			sum+=atr.charCodeAt(i);
		}

		document.getElementById("hOV_response").value = sum;
		/*captcha code end*/
		var target = document.getElementById( $(this).data('target') );
		var clickId = $(this).data('target');

		if(typeof(target) != 'undefined' && target != null && target.value.length > 3)
		{
			$(this).data('click-state', 'clicked');
			var emailTo = target.value;
			$('#basketEmailHidden').val(emailTo);
			jsrAction('saveBasket', emailTo + ',' + clickId);
		}
		else
		{
			if(clickId == 'emailBasketAddress')
				$('#section_reportToUserInline').html('<p class="basketError fw_inputerror">Invalid email input, please retry</p>');
			else
				$('#section_reportToUserPopup').html('<p class="basketError fw_inputerror">Invalid email input, please retry</p>');
		}
	});
});

<script>
/**
 * jquery.wait - insert simple delays into your jquery method chains
 * @author Matthew Lee matt@madleedesign.com
 */

(function ($) {
	function jQueryDummy ($real, delay, _fncQueue) {
		// A Fake jQuery-like object that allows us to resolve the entire jQuery
		// method chain, pause, and resume execution later.

		var dummy = this;
		this._fncQueue = (typeof _fncQueue === "undefined") ? [] : _fncQueue;
		this._delayCompleted = false;
		this._$real = $real;

		if (typeof delay === "number" && delay >= 0 && delay < Infinity)
			this.timeoutKey = window.setTimeout(function () {
				dummy._performDummyQueueActions();
			}, delay);

		else if (delay !== null && typeof delay === "object" && typeof delay.promise === "function")
			delay.then(function () {
				dummy._performDummyQueueActions();
			});

		else if (typeof delay === "string")
			$real.one(delay, function () {
				dummy._performDummyQueueActions();
			});

		else
			return $real;
	}

	jQueryDummy.prototype._addToQueue = function(fnc, arg){
		// When dummy functions are called, the name of the function and
		// arguments are put into a queue to execute later

		this._fncQueue.unshift({ fnc: fnc, arg: arg });

		if (this._delayCompleted)
			return this._performDummyQueueActions();
		else
			return this;
	};

	jQueryDummy.prototype._performDummyQueueActions = function(){
		// Start executing queued actions. If another `wait` is encountered,
		// pass the remaining stack to a new jQueryDummy

		this._delayCompleted = true;

		var next;
		while (this._fncQueue.length > 0) {
			next = this._fncQueue.pop();

			if (next.fnc === "wait") {
				next.arg.push(this._fncQueue);
				return this._$real = this._$real[next.fnc].apply(this._$real, next.arg);
			}

			this._$real = this._$real[next.fnc].apply(this._$real, next.arg);
		}

		return this;
	};

	$.fn.wait = function(delay, _queue) {
		// Creates dummy object that dequeues after a times delay OR promise

		return new jQueryDummy(this, delay, _queue);
	};

	for (var fnc in $.fn) {
		// Add shadow methods for all jQuery methods in existence. Will not
		// shadow methods added to jQuery _after_ this!
		// skip non-function properties or properties of Object.prototype

		if (typeof $.fn[fnc] !== "function" || !$.fn.hasOwnProperty(fnc))
			continue;

		jQueryDummy.prototype[fnc] = (function (fnc) {
			return function(){
				var arg = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
				return this._addToQueue(fnc, arg);
			};
		})(fnc);
	}
})(jQuery);
</script><!--JSLINKEND-->

<script type="text/javascript">
window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
	//console.log('Received message ' + event.data.messageType);
	if(event.data.messageType == 'signup') {
		var obj = JSON.parse(atob(event.data.messagePayload));
		if(obj.status == 'cendynok') {
			$('#top-filter-profile-label').html(obj.nameFull);
			$('#cendyn-logged-in-info').html(obj.content).show();
			$('#cendyn-log-in-form').hide();				
			$('#loggedInIcon').show();
			$('#login_email').val('');
			$('#login_password').val('');
			if(typeof avvioCRMLoginCallback == 'function')
				avvioCRMLoginCallback(obj);
			//setTimeout(function() { closeInlineFrame(); }, 3000);
		}	
	}
	else if(event.data.messageType == 'login') {
		var obj = JSON.parse(atob(event.data.messagePayload));
		if(obj.status == 'success') {
			updateAvvioLoginAreaManual(obj);
			setTimeout(function() {
				closeInlineFrame();
			}, 3000);
		}	
	}
});

var avvio_fct=-1;
$(document).ready(function() {
	
	avvioUpdateScrollMarker();
	if(avvio_fct > -1)
		$(window).scroll(function() { avvioUpdateScroll(); });
	$('<div id="the_lights"></div>').prependTo('body');
	if( $( '#lightsclickdisabled' ).length === 0 ) $('<input id="lightsclickdisabled" type="hidden" value="0" />').appendTo('body');
	avvioUpdateScroll();
	$('#the_lights').click(function()
	{
		if($('#lightsclickdisabled').val() == 1)
			return;
		if(imagecycletimeout) clearInterval(imagecycletimeout);
		if(typeof closePopup == 'function')
			closePopup()
		else
		{
			$('#popupdiv').fadeOut('fast'); lightsOn();
		}
	});

	// $( '#ipulse .navigation-box' ).on( 'click', function() { $(this).toggleClass( 'navigation-show' ); });
	var isTouch = (('ontouchstart' in window) || (navigator.msMaxTouchPoints > 0));
	if( ! isTouch)
		$('body').addClass('no-touch');

	if( navigator.userAgent.match( /(iPod|iPhone|iPad)/ ) ) {
		var body = jQuery( 'body' );

		$(document)
			.on( 'focus', 'input:not( [type="button"] ):not( [type="radio"] ):not( [type="checkbox"] ), textarea', function( e ) {
				body.addClass( 'fixfixed' );
			})
			.on( 'blur', 'input, textarea', function( e ) {
				body.removeClass( 'fixfixed' );
			});
	}
	
	$(document).trigger( 'avvioTemplateDocReadyLate' );
});

function avvioUpdateScrollMarker()
{
	var fcc = $('#fixedcontent_container');
	if(fcc.length > 0)
		avvio_fct = fcc.offset().top;
}

function toggleMenuOption(option)
{
	// $('#login_popup').hide();
	$('#signup_popup').hide();
	$('.opt_arrow').hide();
	if($('#menuoptionsdiv_'+option).is(':visible'))
	{
		$('#menuoptionsdiv_'+option).slideUp(100);
		return;
	}
	else
	{
		$('.menuoptionsdiv').hide();
		$('#menuoptionsdiv_'+option).slideDown(100);
		$('#opt_arrow_'+option).show();
	}
}

function b64DecodeUnicode(str) {
    return decodeURIComponent(atob(str).split('').map(function(c) {
        return '%' + ('00' + c.charCodeAt(0).toString(16)).slice(-2);
    }).join(''));
}

function openInlineFrame(title,source,className)
{
	className = (typeof className !== 'undefined') ? className : '';
	$('#inlineFrameContainer').removeClass();
	$('#inlineFrameContainer').addClass(className);
	$('#inlineFrame').attr('src','data:text/html, <div style="font:11px arial;padding:20px;">Loading...</div>');
	$( '#ipulse .top-filter-container .top-filter-button-active' ).first().trigger( 'click' );
	lightsOff(true);
	$('#frameTitle').html(b64DecodeUnicode(title));
	$('#inlineFrame').attr('src', b64DecodeUnicode(source));
	$('#inlineFrameContainer').fadeIn(100);
}
function closeInlineFrame()
{
	$('#inlineFrame').attr('src','data:text/html, <div style="font:11px arial;padding:20px;">&nbsp;</div>');
	$('#inlineFrameContainer').fadeOut(100);
	lightsOn(true);
}

function avvioUpdateScroll()
{
	return 1;
}
function lightsOff( clicksdisabled )
{
	if( clicksdisabled === undefined ) clicksdisabled = false;

	if( clicksdisabled )
		$( '#lightsclickdisabled' ).val( '1' );

	$( '#the_lights' ).addClass( 'lightsdark' );
	$( 'html' ).addClass( 'non-scrolling' );

	$(document).trigger( 'lightsOff' );
}
function lightsOn( clicksenabled )
{
	if( clicksenabled === undefined ) clicksenabled = false;

	if( clicksenabled )
		$( '#lightsclickdisabled' ).val( '0' );

	$('#inlineFrameContainer').hide();
	$( '#the_lights' ).removeClass( 'lightsdark' );
	$( 'html' ).removeClass( 'non-scrolling' );
	$('.footer-component-disabled').removeClass('footer-component-disabled');

	$(document).trigger( 'lightsOn' );
}

function showLoginPopupLayer()
{
	$('.menuoptionsdiv').hide();
	$('.opt_arrow').hide();
	// $('#login_popup').fadeIn(100);
}

function hideLoginPopupLayer()
{
	// $('#login_popup').fadeOut(100);
	$('#async_login_message').html('');
}

function updateAvvioLoginAreaManual(obj)
{
	var greet = '';
	if(obj.nameFirst.length > 1) greet = obj.nameFirst;
	else if(obj.email.length > 1) greet = obj.email;

	$('.loggedoutlink').hide();
	$('.loggedinlink').show();

	var welcome = 'Welcome _EMAIL_, you are now logged in';
	welcome = welcome.replace('_EMAIL_', greet);
	var msg = '<div id="loginmessage" class="success">' + welcome + '</div>';

	$('#async_login_message').html(msg);

	var det = '';
	if(obj.nameFull) det += (obj.nameFull + '<br/>');
	det += obj.email;

	$('#login_userdetails').html(det);

	$('#optlink_userid').attr('title', obj.email + ' logged in');

	$('#login_changedetails').attr('href', 'https://secure.kilkennyormonde.com/crm/site/Kilkenny Ormonde Hotel/en/change_login_profile.html');
	$('#login_logout').attr('href', 'javascript:doCRMLogout();');

	$('#login_login').css('display','none');
	$('#login_requestaccount').css('display','none');

	$('#isloggedin').css('visibility','visible');

	$('.avvio-logged-in-container').css('visibility','visible');
	$('.avvio-liu-first-name').html(obj.nameFirst);
	$('.avvio-liu-email').html(obj.email);

	setTimeout('hideLoginPopupLayer()', 2000);

	if(typeof avvioCRMLoginCallback == 'function')
		avvioCRMLoginCallback(obj);

	$( '#login_popup' ).trigger( 'avvioCRMLogin', obj );
	$( '#avvio_login' ).trigger( 'avvioCRMLogin', obj );
}

function doCRMLogin()
{
	$('#loginloading').css('visibility','visible');
	$.ajax({
		url: "https://secure.kilkennyormonde.com/crm/site/Kilkenny Ormonde Hotel/en/login.html",
		type: "post",
		xhrFields: { withCredentials: true },
		//data: $('#template_login').serialize() + '&fw_jsrequest=crmlogin&fw_submitted=1',
		data: $('#login_email, #login_password').serialize() + '&fw_jsrequest=crmlogin&fw_submitted=1',
		error: function (result) {
			ajaxrunning=0;
			$('#loginloading').css('visibility','hidden');
			//console.log('login Error. ' + JSON.stringify(result));
		},

		success: function (result, textStatus, x) {
			//console.log('login Success. ' + JSON.stringify(result));
			$('#loginloading').css('visibility','hidden');
			var obj={};
			if(result != '')
			{
				try
				{
					var obj = JSON.parse(result);
				}
				catch(err) {
					$('#async_login_message').html('<div id="loginmessage" class="error">Technical Error</div>');
				}
			}
			if(obj.status == 'error')
			{
				var msg = '<div id="loginmessage" class="error">' + obj.errorTexts.join('<br/>') + '</div>';
				$('#async_login_message').html(msg);
			}
			else if(obj.status == 'success')
			{
				updateAvvioLoginAreaManual(obj);
			}
			else if(obj.status == 'cendynok') {				
				$('#top-filter-profile-label').html(obj.nameFull);
				$('#cendyn-logged-in-info').html(obj.content).show();
				$('#cendyn-log-in-form').hide();				
				$('#loggedInIcon').show();
				$('#login_email').val('');
				$('#login_password').val('');
				if(typeof avvioCRMLoginCallback == 'function')
					avvioCRMLoginCallback(obj);					
				setTimeout(function() {
					$( '#ipulse .top-filter-container .top-filter-button-active' ).first().trigger( 'click' );
				}, 2000);
			}
		}
	});
}

function resetCRMPassword()
{
	$.ajax({
		url: "https://secure.kilkennyormonde.com/crm/site/Kilkenny Ormonde Hotel/en/login.html",
		type: "post",
		//data: $('#template_login').serialize() + '&fw_jsrequest=crmRequestPassword&fw_submitted=1',
		data: $('#login_email, #login_password').serialize() + '&fw_jsrequest=crmRequestPassword&currentLanguage=english&fw_submitted=1',
		error: function (result) {
			ajaxrunning=0;
		},
		success: function (result, textStatus, x) {
			var obj={};
			if(result != '')
			{
				try
				{
					eval('var obj='+result+';');
				}
				catch(err) {
					var msg = '<div id="loginmessage" class="error">A technical error has occurred.</div>';
					$('#async_login_message').html(msg);

				}
			}
			if (obj.status == 'error')
			{
				var msg = '<div id="loginmessage" class="error">' + obj.errorTexts.join('<br/>') + '</div>';
				$('#async_login_message').html(msg);
			}
			else if (obj.status == 'success')
			{
				var msg = '<div id="loginmessage" class="success">' + obj.message + '</div>';
				$('#async_login_message').html(msg);
				setTimeout('hideLoginPopupLayer()', 4000);
			}
		}
	});
}

function doCRMLogout()
{
	$.ajax({
		url: "https://secure.kilkennyormonde.com/crm/site/Kilkenny Ormonde Hotel/en/logout.html?fw_jsrequest=crmlogout",
		type: "get",
		xhrFields: { withCredentials: true },
		data: null,
		error: function (result) {
			ajaxrunning=0;
		},

		success: function (result, textStatus, x) {
			var obj={};
			if(result != '')
			{
				try
				{
					var obj = JSON.parse(result);
				}
				catch(err) {
					$('#async_login_message').html('<div id="loginmessage" class="error">Technical Error</div>');
				}
			}
			if(obj.status == 'ok')
			{
				$('.loggedinlink').hide();
				$('.loggedoutlink').show();

				$('.avvio-logged-in-container').css('visibility','hidden');
				$('#login_userdetails').html('You are not logged in');
				$('.menuoptionsdiv').hide();
				$('#opt_arrow_login').hide();
				$('#isloggedin').css('visibility','hidden');
				if(typeof avvioCRMLogoutCallback == 'function')
					avvioCRMLogoutCallback(obj);

				$( '#login_popup' ).trigger( 'avvioCRMLogout' );
				$( '#avvio_login' ).trigger( 'avvioCRMLogout' );
			}
			else if(obj.status == 'cendynok') {
				$('#top-filter-profile-label').html('');
				$('#cendyn-logged-in-info').hide();
				$('#login_email').val('');
				$('#login_password').val('');
				$('#cendyn-log-in-form').show();				
				$('#loggedInIcon').hide();
				if(typeof avvioCRMLogoutCallback == 'function')
					avvioCRMLogoutCallback(obj);	
				setTimeout(function() {
					$( '#ipulse .top-filter-container .top-filter-button-active' ).first().trigger( 'click' );
				}, 300);
			}
		}
	});
}
function isKeydownAndEnterEvent( event )
{
	if( event.type == 'keydown' )
	{
		var keycode = event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which;
		if( keycode == '13' )
			return true;
		return false;
	}
	return true;
}
